#### <a name="officetargetedmessagingensurecached"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-492">Office.TargetedMessaging.EnsureCached</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-492">Office.TargetedMessaging.EnsureCached</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-493">Seka, ar buvo atsisiųstas paketas dinaminei matomosios tinklalapio srities daliai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-493">Tracks if a package for Dynamic Canvas was downloaded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-494">Laikoma taikomosios programinės įrangos konfigūracija, nes paketas turi būti sėkmingai atsisiųstas, kad įgalinti klientą generuoti tinkamą patirtį.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-494">Considered a software configuration because the package must be successfully downloaded to enable the client to render the right experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-495">Yra ypač kritinės vartotojo prenumeratoms, kur matomąją tinklalapio sritį naudojame informuoti vartotoją, kad licencija nebegalioja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-495">Is especially critical in consumer subscriptions where we use canvas to communicate to the user that the license has expired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-496">Naudojamas sekti metaduomenis dinaminio turinio paketo, kurį atsisiuntė ir į talpyklą įkėlė produktas, taip pat operacijų, atliktų su paketu, rezultatus: nesėkmingus atsisiuntimus, negalimą išsipakavimą, nuolatines patikros triktis, sėkmingą kreipimąsi į talpyklą, paketo naudojimus ir atsisiuntimo šaltinius.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-496">Used to track metadata of a dynamic content package downloaded and cached by the product as well as results of operations performed on the package: download failures, unpacking failures, consistency checks failures, cache hits, package usages, download sources.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-497">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-497">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-498">**Data\_CacheFolderNotCreated –** Bulio logikos žyma nurodo, ar pavyko sukurti talpyklos aplanką</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-498">**Data\_CacheFolderNotCreated -** Boolean flag indicating if cache folder creation succeed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-499">**Data\_CdnPath – paketo šaltinio adresas –**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-499">**Data\_CdnPath – source address of the package-**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-500">**Data\_EnsureCached –** Bulio logikos žyma, nurodanti, ar turinio paketas buvo įtrauktas į talpyklą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-500">**Data\_EnsureCached -** Boolean flag indicating if content package was cached</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-501">**Data\_ExistsAlready –** Bulio logikos žyma, nurodanti, kad paketas jau buvo atsisiųstas anksčiau ir buvo dar vienas bandymas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-501">**Data\_ExistsAlready -** Boolean flag indicating that the package was already downloaded before and there was another attempt</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-502">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailed –** šaltinio paketo nėra šaltinyje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-502">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailed -** source package not available in source</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-503">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailedToCreateLocalFolder –** vietinio disko problemos, dėl kurių nepavyksta sukurti katalogo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-503">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailedToCreateLocalFolder -** local disk issues causing failure in directory creation</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-504">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageFailed –** žyma, nurodanti, ar paketas buvo atsisiųstas, bet klientas negali jo perskaityti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-504">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageFailed -** flag indicating if package was downloaded, but the client can’t read it</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-505">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageSuccess –** sėkmingi paketo perskaitymo bandymai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-505">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageSuccess -** successful attempts to read the package</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-506">**Data\_GetFileStreamSuccess -** nėra disko arba konfigūravimo problemų, neleidžiančių skaityti failų srautą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-506">**Data\_GetFileStreamSuccess -** no disk issues nor configuration issues which doesn’t let the file stream to be read</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-507">**Data\_GetRelativePathsFailed –** santykinis kelias nenurodo pasiekiamos vietos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-507">**Data\_GetRelativePathsFailed -** relative path doesn’t point to accessible location</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-508">**Data\_HashActualValue –** maišos vertė paimta iš failo pavadinimo paketo naudojimo metu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-508">**Data\_HashActualValue -** hash value extracted from file name when the package was used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-509">**Data\_HashCalculationFailed –** maišos skaičiavimo klaida</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-509">**Data\_HashCalculationFailed -** error with calculation of a hash</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-510">**Data\_HashMatchFailed –** maišos neatitikimas tarp paketo pavadinimo ir registro vertės, įtrauktos į talpyklą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-510">**Data\_HashMatchFailed -** hash mismatch between the package name and registry values cached</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-511">**Data\_HashMatchSuccess –** sėkminga maišos nuoseklumo patikra</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-511">**Data\_HashMatchSuccess -** hash consistency check success</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-512">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestFailed –** negalima atsisiųsti paketo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-512">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestFailed -** can’t download the package</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-513">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestNoData –** atsisiųstame pakete nėra duomenų</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-513">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestNoData -** downloaded package contains no data</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-514">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestSuccess –** sėkmingas paketo atsisiuntimas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-514">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestSuccess -** successful download of a package</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-515">**Data\_PackageExplodedSuccess –** bandymo išpakuoti būsenos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-515">**Data\_PackageExplodedSuccess -** unpacking attempts statuses</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-516">**Data\_PackageOpenFailed –** nepavykę bandymai atidaryti paketo failą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-516">**Data\_PackageOpenFailed -** failed attempts to open the package file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-517">**Data\_PackageOpenSuccess –** pavykę bandymai atidaryti paketo failą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-517">**Data\_PackageOpenSuccess -** successful attempts to open the package file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-518">**Data\_SuccessHashValue –** maišos vertė paimta iš failo pavadinimo, kai buvo atsisiųstas paketas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-518">**Data\_SuccessHashValue -** hash value extracted from file name when the package was downloaded</span></span>

#### <a name="officefileiocsiccachedfilecsisavefilebasic"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-933">Office.FileIO.CSI.CCachedFileCsiSaveFileBasic</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-933">Office.FileIO.CSI.CCachedFileCsiSaveFileBasic</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-934">Leidžia mums žinoti, ar failas iš FIO sluoksnio įrašytas sėkmingai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-934">Allows us to know if a file was successfully saved from the FIO Layer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-935">Naudojama funkcijos sveikatai užtikrinti ir stebėti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-935">Used for Feature Health and monitoring.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-936">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-936">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-937">**Activity.Group –** žymė, leidžianti nustatyti stebimų įvykių rinkinį, grupuojamą sėkmingam atlikimui valdyti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-937">**Activity.Group -** tag that allows a set of monitoring events to be grouped to manage overall success</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-938">**Activity.IsHVA –** žyma, nurodanti, kad įvykis yra kritinis vartotojų sėkmingiems veiksmams užtikrinti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-938">**Activity.IsHVA -** flag to indicate that event is critical to user success</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-939">**Data.AsyncOpen –** žyma, nurodanti, kad dokumentas buvo atidarytas su turiniu, gautu po pagrindinės dalies atidarymo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-939">**Data.AsyncOpen -** flag to indicate that the document was opened with content that arrived after the main body was opened</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-940">**Data.BaseDownloadTriggered –** keičia sekimo diagnostiką, nurodančią, kad buvo užklausta pagrindinė dokumento versija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-940">**Data.BaseDownloadTriggered -** Change tracking diagnostic indicating that the base version of the document was requested</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-941">**Data.BlockAutoUploadReasons –** užblokuotos nusiuntimo būsenos priežasčių kodai (pvz. automatinis įrašymas išjungtas, dokumentas perkeliamas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-941">**Data.BlockAutoUploadReasons -** Reason codes for blocked upload state (e.g. Autosave is turned off, the document is transitioning)</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-942">**Data.BlockUploadDueToFailedSaveAsOverExisting –** nusiuntimas užblokuotas, nes kartojant jis nepavyks</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-942">**Data.BlockUploadDueToFailedSaveAsOverExisting -** Upload is blocked as it would fail if retried</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-943">**Data.CacheFileId –** prisijungia prie „Office“ dokumentų talpyklos telemetrijos, kad atliktų vartotojo patiriamų talpyklos problemų analizę</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-943">**Data.CacheFileId -** connects to Office Document Cache telemetry to enable impact analysis of cache issues on the user experience</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-944">**Data.ChartType –** nebenaudojamas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-944">**Data.ChartType -** Obsolete</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationnewdocument"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-1213">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.NewDocument</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1213">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.NewDocument</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1214">Surinkta, „PowerPoint“ naujos pateikties sukūrimo metu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1214">Collected when PowerPoint creates a new presentation.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="6e043-1215"> Apima sėkmingą klaidos šalinimą ir našumo metrikas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1215"> Includes success failure and performance metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1216">Ši informacija naudojama užtikrinti, kad galime sukurti failus sėkmingai, nemažinant našumo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1216">This information is used to ensure we can create files successfully and with no degradation in performance.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1217">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1217">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1218">**NewDocumentType** – ar naujas dokumentas sukurtas naudojant šabloną, ar sukurtas tik tuščias dokumentas?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1218">**NewDocumentType** – Whether new document is created from template or just created blank?</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1219">**FLifeguarded** – dokumento apsauga (funkcija, atkurianti sugadintos būsenos dokumentą nepateikdami raginimo vartotojui)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1219">**FLifeguarded** – Is document life guarded (feature that restores corrupt document state without prompting user)</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationopencompleteprotocol"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-1220">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.OpenCompleteProtocol</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1220">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.OpenCompleteProtocol</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1221">Surinkta „PowerPoint“ atidarius pateiktis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1221">Collected when PowerPoint opens presentations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1222">Joje yra informacija, reikalinga tinkamai nustatyti ir diagnozuoti problemas, įvykusias atidarymo proceso baigiamosiose stadijose.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1222">It contains the information needed to be able to properly investigate and diagnose issues that happen through the end stages of the open process.</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsave"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-1279">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Save</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1279">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Save</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1280">Surinkti kiekvieną kartą, kai „PowerPoint“ įrašo naudodama modernų kodo kelią.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1280">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a save using the modern code path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1281">Apima sėkmingai arba nesėkmingai atlikto našumo metrikų ir susijusio dokumento metaduomenų įrašymo rezultato tipą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1281">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1282"> Nepavykus įrašymui, duomenys gali būti prarasti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1282"> Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1283">„Microsoft“ naudoja šiuos duomenis, kad užtikrintų, jog funkcija veikia kaip priklauso ir vartotojo turinys yra sėkmingai išlaikomas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1283">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsaveas"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-1364">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveAs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1364">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveAs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1365">Surinkti kiekvieną kartą, kai „PowerPoint“ atlieka operaciją įrašyti kaip.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1365">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a Save As.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1366">Apima sėkmingai arba nesėkmingai atlikto našumo metrikų ir susijusio dokumento metaduomenų įrašymo rezultato tipą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1366">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1367">Nepavykus įrašymui, duomenys gali būti prarasti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1367">Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1368">„Microsoft“ naudoja šiuos duomenis, kad užtikrintų, jog funkcija veikia kaip priklauso ir vartotojo turinys yra sėkmingai išlaikomas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1368">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1369">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1369">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1370">**Data\_AddDocTelemetryResult:long –** ar šis žurnalo įrašas turi visą reikiamą dokumento telemetriją (Data\_Doc\_\* laukus)?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1370">**Data\_AddDocTelemetryResult:long -** Does this log entry have all necessary document telemetry (Data\_Doc\_\* fields)?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1371">Jei ne, kodėl?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1371">If not, why?</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1372">**Data\_CppUncaughtExceptionCount:long –** veiklos veikimo metu neaptiktos vietinės išimtys</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1372">**Data\_CppUncaughtExceptionCount:long -** Uncaught native exceptions while activity was running</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1373">**Data\_DetachedDuration:long –** veiklos atskyrimo / neveikimo trukmė</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1373">**Data\_DetachedDuration:long -** Time for which Activity was detached/not running</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1374">**Data\_DstDoc\_AccessMode:long –** kaip šis dokumentas buvo atidarytas (tik skaityti | skaityti ir rašyti)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1374">**Data\_DstDoc\_AccessMode:long -** How was this document opened (Read only | read write)</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1375">**Data\_DstDoc\_AccessMode:long –** iš anksto apibrėžtų reikšmių, nurodančių dokumento atidarymo pagalbiniu skaitymo režimu priežastis, rinkinys</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1375">**Data\_DstDoc\_AssistedReadingReasons:long -** Predefined set of values of why document was opened in assisted reading mode</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1376">**Data\_DstDoc\_ChunkingType:long –** kaip dokumentas saugomas programoje „SharePoint“</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1376">**Data\_DstDoc\_ChunkingType:long -** How is document stored in SharePoint</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1377">**Data\_DstDoc\_EdpState:long –** dokumento įmonės duomenų apsaugos būsena</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1377">**Data\_DstDoc\_EdpState:long -** Enterprise Data Protection state of document</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1378">**Data\_DstDoc\_Ext:string –** dokumento plėtinys</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1378">**Data\_DstDoc\_Ext:string -** Document extension</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1379">**Data\_DstDoc\_Extension:string –** dokumento plėtinys</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1379">**Data\_DstDoc\_Extension:string -** Document extension</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1380">**Data\_DstDoc\_FileFormat:long –** iš anksto nustatytų failo formato reikšmių rinkinys (detalesnis nei plėtinio)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1380">**Data\_DstDoc\_FileFormat:long -** Predefined set of values of format of file (more granular than extension)</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1381">**Data\_DstDoc\_Fqdn:string –** vieta, kurioje saugomas dokumentas (SharePoint.com, live.net) galima tik „Office 365“ domenams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1381">**Data\_DstDoc\_Fqdn:string -** Where is document stored (SharePoint.com, live.net), only available for Office 365 domains</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1382">**Data\_DstDoc\_FqdnHash:string –** dokumento saugojimo vietos maiša</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1382">**Data\_DstDoc\_FqdnHash:string -** Hash of where document is stored</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1383">**Data\_DstDoc\_IdentityTelemetryId:string –** unikalus vartotojo GUID</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1383">**Data\_DstDoc\_IdentityTelemetryId:string -** Unique GUID of user</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsavelegacy"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-1459">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveLegacy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1459">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveLegacy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1460">Surinkti kiekvieną kartą, kai „PowerPoint“ įrašo naudodama senesnį kodo kelią.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1460">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a save using the legacy code path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1461">Apima sėkmingai arba nesėkmingai atlikto našumo metrikų ir susijusio dokumento metaduomenų įrašymo rezultato tipą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1461">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1462">Nepavykus įrašymui, duomenys gali būti prarasti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1462">Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1463">„Microsoft“ naudoja šiuos duomenis, kad užtikrintų, jog funkcija veikia kaip priklauso ir vartotojo turinys yra sėkmingai išlaikomas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1463">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1798">Šis įvykis registruoja dokumentų statistiką kiekvienam dokumentui, kai „Office Word“ yra uždaryta ar sustabdyta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1798">This event logs document statistics for each document when Office Word is closed or suspended.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfilenewcreatenewfile"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-1829">Office.Word.FileNew.CreateNewFile</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1829">Office.Word.FileNew.CreateNewFile</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1830">Šis įvykis nurodo, kad sukurtas naujas dokumentas „Office Word“ ir sekamas sėkmingas arba nesėkmingas operacijų atlikimas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1830">This event indicates that a new document is created in Office Word and tracks success or failure of the operation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1831">Įvykis naudojamas stebėti, ar naujų dokumentų kūrimas veikia tinkamai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1831">The event is used to monitor that new document creation is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1832">Jis taip pat naudojamas mėnesio aktyviems vartotojams / įrenginiams ir debesies patikimumo rodikliams apskaičiuoti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1832">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1833">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1833">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1834">**Data\_DirtyState** – ar dokumentas buvo sukurtas neatnaujintoje būsenoje (su pakeitimais, kurie turi būti įrašyti)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1834">**Data\_DirtyState** - whether the document was created in a dirty state (with changes that need to be saved)</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfilesaveactcmdgosubsaveas"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-1838">Office.Word.FileSave.ActCmdGosubSaveAs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1838">Office.Word.FileSave.ActCmdGosubSaveAs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1839">Šis įvykis nurodo, kad vartotojas įrašo savo pakeitimus į naują dokumentą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1839">This event indicates that a user is saving their changes to a new document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1840">Įvykis stebi, ar įrašymas į naują dokumentą veikia tinkamai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1840">The event monitors whether saving to a new document is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1841">Jis taip pat naudojamas mėnesio aktyviems vartotojams / įrenginiams ir debesies patikimumo rodikliams apskaičiuoti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1841">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfilesaveactfconfirmsavedoccoreautorecoverysave"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-1887">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreAutoRecoverySave</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1887">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreAutoRecoverySave</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1888">Šis įvykis nurodo, kad „Office Word“ įrašo automatinio atkūrimo dokumentą, kuris anksčiau nebuvo įrašytas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1888">This event indicates Office Word saves an auto-recovery document that has not been saved before.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1889">Tai suteikia galimybę „Microsoft“ aptikti automatinio atkūrimo klaidas, svarbias dokumento duomenų saugumui.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1889">It allows Microsoft to detect errors in auto-recovery which is important for document data safety.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1890">Įvykis stebi, ar automatinio atkūrimo įrašymo funkcija veikia tinkamai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1890">The event monitors whether auto-recovery-save is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1891">Jis taip pat naudojamas mėnesio aktyviems vartotojams / įrenginiams ir debesies patikimumo rodikliams apskaičiuoti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1891">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1892">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1892">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1894">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode –** dokumentas yra skirtas tik skaityti / redaguoti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1894">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode -** Document is read only/editable</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1898">**Data\_Doc\_Ext –** dokumento plėtinys (docx / xlsb / pptx ir kt.)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1898">**Data\_Doc\_Ext -** Document extension (docx/xlsb/pptx etc.)</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfilesaveactfconfirmsavedoccorequerysave"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-1937">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreQuerySave</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1937">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreQuerySave</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1938">Šis įvykis nurodo, kad „Office Word“ ragina vartotoją įrašyti keitimus, kai programa bando uždaryti dokumentą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1938">This event indicates Office Word prompts the user to save changes when it tries to close the document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1939">Tai leidžia „Microsoft“ stebėti, ar įrašymas išėjimo metu veikia tinkamai, kad neprarasti dokumento duomenų.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1939">It allows Microsoft to monitor whether save-at-quit works as expected to avoid document data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1940">Įvykis stebi, ar funkcija įrašyti išėjimo metu veikia tinkamai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1940">The event monitors whether save-at-quit is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-1941">Jis taip pat naudojamas mėnesio aktyviems vartotojams / įrenginiams ir debesies patikimumo rodikliams apskaičiuoti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1941">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfilesavesaveassavefile"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-1998">Office.Word.FileSave.SaveAsSaveFile</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1998">Office.Word.FileSave.SaveAsSaveFile</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-1999">Šis įvykis nurodo, kad „Office Word“ įrašo dokumentą į naują dokumentą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-1999">This event indicates Office Word saves a document into a new document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2000">Tai leidžia „Microsoft“ aptikti funkcijos Įrašyti kaip klaidas, o tai svarbu norint išvengti dokumento duomenų praradimo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2000">It allows Microsoft to detect errors in save-as which is important to avoid document data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2001">Įvykis stebi, ar funkcija Įrašyti kaip veikia tinkamai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2001">The event monitors whether save-as is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2002">Jis taip pat naudojamas mėnesio aktyviems vartotojams / įrenginiams ir debesies patikimumo rodikliams apskaičiuoti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2002">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordworddocumentdirtyflagchanged"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-2120">Office.Word.Word.DocumentDirtyFlagChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2120">Office.Word.Word.DocumentDirtyFlagChanged</span></span>

#### <a name="officevisiosharedfeatureexperimentation"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-2136">Office.Visio.Shared.FeatureExperimentation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2136">Office.Visio.Shared.FeatureExperimentation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2137">Stebi funkcijos testavimą vartotojams.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2137">Tracks feature flighting for users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2138">Šis įvykis padės mums nustatyti, ar funkcija testuojama sėkmingai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2138">This event helps us determines success or failure of feature flights.</span></span>

#### <a name="officeprojectopenproject"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-2566">Office.Project.OpenProject</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2566">Office.Project.OpenProject</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2567">„Project“ atidaro failą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2567">Project opens a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2568">Šis įvykis nurodo vartotojui, kad jis tiesiogiai atidaro „Project“ failą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2568">This event indicates a user directly opening a Project file by a user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2569">Jame yra svarbūs duomenys, užtikrinantys, kad „Project“ bus sėkmingai atidaromi failai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2569">It contains critical success data of opening files in Project.</span></span>

#### <a name="officesessionidproviderofficeprocesssessionstart"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-2581">Office.SessionIdProvider.OfficeProcessSessionStart</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2581">Office.SessionIdProvider.OfficeProcessSessionStart</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2582">Taikoma visoms „Office“ „Windows“ pagrįstomis programomis: win32 ir UWP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2582">Applicable to all the Office windows-based applications: win32 and UWP</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2583">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2583">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2584">**OfficeProcessSessionStart** Siunčia pagrindinę informaciją į naują „Office“ seanso pradžią.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2584">**OfficeProcessSessionStart** sends basic information upon the start of a new Office session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2585">Naudojamas norint suskaičiuoti unikalius seansus, matomus šiais įrenginiais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2585">This is used to count the number of unique sessions seen on a given device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2586">Jis naudojamas kaip pasikartojantis įvykis, kad užtikrintų, jog taikomoji programa paleista įrenginyje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2586">This is used as a heartbeat event to ensure that the application is running on a device or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2587">Be to, tai yra svarbus visos programos patikimumo signalas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2587">In addition, it serves as a critical signal for overall application reliability</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2588">**ProgramosSeansoVedikl** – konkrečios taikomosios programos seanso pradžios identifikatorius, naudojamas nuo proceso kūrimo pradžios ir iki proceso pabaigos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2588">**AppSessionGuid** - An identifier of a particular application session starting at process creation time and persisting until process end.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2589">Jis yra suformuotas kaip standartinis 128 bitų GUID, tik sudarytas iš 4 dalių.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2589">It is formatted as a standard 128-bit GUID but constructed of 4 parts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2590">Šios keturios dalys eil4s tvarka yra (1) 32 bitų proceso ID (2) 16 bitų seanso ID (3) 16 bitų įkrovos ID (4) 64 bitų proceso sukūrimo laikasm išreikštas UTC 100ns</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2590">Those four parts in order are (1) 32 bit Process ID (2) 16 bit Session ID (3) 16 bit Boot ID (4) 64 bit Process creation time in UTC 100ns</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2591">**processSessionId** - Atsitiktinai sugeneruotas žinynas, skirtas programos seansui identifikuoti </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2591">**processSessionId** - Randomly generated guid to identify the app session</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2592">**UTCReplace_AppSessionGuid** - Pastovi Bulio logikos vertė.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2592">**UTCReplace_AppSessionGuid** - Constant boolean value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2593">Visuomet „True“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2593">Always true.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2661">**Data\_Doc\_UrlHash –** vienpusė maiša, skirta „naïve“ dokumento identifikatoriui</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2661">**Data\_Doc\_UrlHash -** One-way hash to create a naïve document identifier</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenffileopenxstzcore"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-2681">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenFFileOpenXstzCore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2681">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenFFileOpenXstzCore</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2682">Šis įvykis nurodo, kad „Office Word“ atidaro dokumentą, kurį vartotojas dukart spustelėjo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2682">This event indicates Office Word opens a document who is double clicked by a user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2683">Jame taip pat yra svarbūs failo atidarymo našumo duomenys ir yra programėlės pradžios įvykis vertinant iš vartotojo perspektyvos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2683">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2684">Įvykis stebi, ar file-open-from-file-double-click veikia tinkamai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2684">The event monitors whether file-open-from-file-double-click is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2685">Jis taip pat naudojamas mėnesio aktyviems vartotojams / įrenginiams ir debesies patikimumo rodikliams apskaičiuoti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2685">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2686">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2686">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2687">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Nurodo, ar įvykyje galima tinkamai užpildyti kitų dokumentų telemetrijos susijusias reikšmes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2687">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Reports whether we were able to properly populate other document telemetry related values in the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2688">Naudojama duomenų kokybės diagnostikai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2688">Used for data quality diagnostics</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2689">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Baitų (suglaudintų), kurie, kaip manoma, gali atidaryti failą, skaičius, nepaisant, ar mes juos gausime, kol vartotojas nori pradėti redaguoti arba galbūt įrašyti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2689">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we believe we can open the file without if we get them before the user wants to start editing or maybe saving</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2690">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork -** Baitų (suglaudintų), kuriuos naudodami galėtume atidaryti failą, skaičius, tačiau norint, kad tai įvyktų, reikės daug investuoti į kodą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2690">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we might be able to open the file without but would require significant code investments to make it happen</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2691">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Baitų (suglaudintų) skaičius, kuriuos privalome turėti prieš pradėdami atidaryti failą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2691">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we must have before we can start opening the file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2692">**Data\_BytesUnknown -** Baitų skaičius dokumentų dalyse, kurių nesitikėjome rasti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2692">**Data\_BytesUnknown -** Number of bytes in document parts that we don’t expect to find</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenifrinitargs"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-2747">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenIfrInitArgs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2747">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenIfrInitArgs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2748">Šis įvykis nurodo, kad „Office Word“ atidaro dokumentą naudojant COM aktyvinimą arba komandinę eilutę.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2748">This event indicates Office Word opens a document via COM activation or command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2749">Jame taip pat yra svarbūs failo atidarymo našumo duomenys ir yra programėlės pradžios įvykis vertinant iš vartotojo perspektyvos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2749">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2750">Įvykis stebi, ar file-open-from-command-line veikia tinkamai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2750">The event monitors whether file-open-from-command-line is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2751">Jis taip pat naudojamas mėnesio aktyviems vartotojams / įrenginiams ir debesies patikimumo rodikliams apskaičiuoti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2751">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2752">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2752">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2753">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes –** nurodo, ar įvykyje galima tinkamai užpildyti kitų dokumentų telemetrijos susijusias reikšmes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2753">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Reports whether we were able to properly populate other document telemetry related values in the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2754">Naudojama duomenų kokybės diagnostikai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2754">Used for data quality diagnostics.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2755">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Baitų (suglaudintų), kurie, kaip manoma, gali atidaryti failą, skaičius, nepaisant, ar mes juos gausime, kol vartotojas nori pradėti redaguoti arba galbūt įrašyti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2755">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we believe we can open the file without if we get them before the user wants to start editing or maybe saving.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2756">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork -** Baitų (suglaudintų), kuriuos naudodami galėtume atidaryti failą, skaičius, tačiau norint, kad tai įvyktų, reikės daug investuoti į kodą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2756">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we might be able to open the file without but would require significant code investments to make it happen</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2757">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Baitų (suglaudintų) skaičius, kuriuos privalome turėti prieš pradėdami atidaryti failą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2757">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we must have before we can start opening the file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2758">**Data\_BytesUnknown -** Baitų skaičius dokumentų dalyse, kurių nesitikėjome rasti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2758">**Data\_BytesUnknown -** Number of bytes in document parts that we don’t expect to find.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2759">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode -** Dokumentas yra skirtas tik skaityti / redaguoti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2759">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode -** Document is read only/editable</span></span>

### <a name="office-accessibility-configuration-subtype"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-2877">*„Office“ pritaikymo neįgaliesiems konfigūracijos potipis*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2877">*Office accessibility configuration subtype*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2878">„Office“ pritaikymo neįgaliesiems funkcijos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2878">Office accessibility features</span></span>

#### <a name="officeaccessibilityaccessibilitytoolsessionpresencewin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-2879">Office.Accessibility.AccessibilityToolSessionPresenceWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2879">Office.Accessibility.AccessibilityToolSessionPresenceWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2880">Leidžia mums nustatyti, ar vartotojas turi pagalbinių technologijų įrankį ir jo pavadinimą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2880">Allows us to detect that the user has an Assistive technology tool and its name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2881">Tai leidžia mums suprasti, ar „Office“ vartotojui kyla konkrečių pagalbinių technologijų įrankio problemų.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2881">This allows us to understand if an Office user is experiencing issues with a specific Assistive Technology tool.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2965">Duomenys aktyviai stebimi, kad būtų pastebėtas neįprastas „pakibimas“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2965">The data is actively monitored for anomalous hangs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2966">Ar jis naudojamas „pakibimams“ aptikti ir identifikuoti, siekiant nustatyti, ką reikia pataisyti būsimuose naujinimuose.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2966">It is used to detect and identify hangs in order to fix in future updates.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-2967">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2967">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-2969">**ElapsedTotal** – bendras iškvietimo laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-2969">**ElapsedTotal** - total time spent in the call</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3385">**Data.CrashHistory System.String** - Struktūra, vaizduojanti vaizdo plokštės tvarkyklės, dėl kurios kilo gedimas, istoriją</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3385">**Data.CrashHistory System.String** - A string that represents the history of video card driver caused crashes for analysis</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3386">**Data.SecsBetweenCrashes** - Kaip dažnai pasitaiko tvarkyklės kortelės gedimų</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3386">**Data.SecsBetweenCrashes** - How frequently driver card crashes are occurring</span></span>

#### <a name="officeairspacebackendwin32localblocklistdriverupdatedactivity"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-3387">Office.AirSpace.Backend.Win32.LocalBlocklistDriverUpdatedActivity</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3387">Office.AirSpace.Backend.Win32.LocalBlocklistDriverUpdatedActivity</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-3388">Vartotojas atnaujino vaizdo plokštės tvarkyklę, kuri anksčiau sukėlė „Office“ gedimus ir todėl nebenaudojama.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3388">User has updated a video card driver that was previously causing Office crashes and thus no longer being used to render.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3389">Informuoja „Microsoft“, kad vartotojai, kurie vieną kartą buvo netinkamoje vaizdo generavimo būsenoje, vėl yra rekomenduojamoje vaizdo generavimo būsenoje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3389">Informs Microsoft that users who were once in a sub-optimal rendering state are once again in the recommended rendering state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-3390">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3390">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3391">**Data\_BlockedDeviceId** – Vaizdo plokštės įrenginio, kuris buvo blokuotas, identifikatorius</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3391">**Data\_BlockedDeviceId** - identifier of the video card device that was blocklisted</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3392">**Data\_BlockedDriverVersion** - Tvarkyklės versija, kuri buvo blokuota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3392">**Data\_BlockedDriverVersion** - Version of the driver that was blocklisted</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3393">**Data\_UpdatedDriverVersion** – Atnaujintos tvarkyklės versija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3393">**Data\_UpdatedDriverVersion** - Version of the updated driver</span></span>

#### <a name="officegraphicsspritememcorrupt"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-3394">Office.Graphics.SpriteMemCorrupt</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3394">Office.Graphics.SpriteMemCorrupt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-3395">Praneša apie aptiktas „sprite“ atminties apskaitos telemetrijos klaidas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3395">Reports any errors detected in the sprite memory accounting telemetry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3396">Svarbu vertinant grafinės atminties naudojimo telemetrijos būseną.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3396">Critical for assessing health of the graphics memory usage telemetry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3397">Ši informacija reikalinga norint patikrinti mūsų „SpriteMem“ telemetrijos tikslumą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3397">This information is needed to validate the correctness of our SpriteMem telemetry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-3398">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3398">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3399">**Duomenų\_CurrentSpriteMem** - Bendras atminties kiekis, aktyviai paskirstytas išlaikyti „sprites“ (vaizdus), dėl kurių atsiranda ekrano turinys.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3399">**Data\_CurrentSpriteMem** - Total amount of memory that is actively allocated to hold sprites (images) that result in screen content.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3400">**Data\_Function** - Funkcijos, kuri bando paleisti „sprite“ atmintį, pavadinimas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3400">**Data\_Function** - The name of the function that is attempting to release sprite memory.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3401">**Data\_SpriteMemToRemove** – Atminties kiekis, kuris turi būti pašalintas iš priskyrimo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3401">**Data\_SpriteMemToRemove** - Amount of memory to be removed from sprite allocation.</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointpptsharednointernetconnectivity"></a><span data-ttu-id="6e043-3402">Office.PowerPoint.PPT.Shared.NoInternetConnectivity</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3402">Office.PowerPoint.PPT.Shared.NoInternetConnectivity</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-3403">Renkama, kai „PowerPoint“ aptinka, kad nėra interneto ryšio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3403">Collected whenever PowerPoint detects there is no internet connectivity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3404">„Microsoft“ naudoja šiuos duomenis, kad gautų diagnostinę informaciją apie vartotojo interneto ryšį, kad galėtų suprasti, kokią tai daro įtaką ryšiui su „Office“ paslaugomis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3404">Microsoft uses this data to get diagnostic information about the user's internet connection to be able to understand how that impacts connectivity to Office services.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6e043-3405">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3405">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6e043-3406">**Data\_IsNexusDetected:bool** - Rodo, ar turime interneto ryšio būseną skambinant „Nexus“ tarnybai (reikšmė TRUE (teisinga) arba iškviečiant bendrosios žiniatinklio tarnybos API iškvietimą (reikšmė FALSE (klaidinga)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6e043-3406">**Data\_IsNexusDetected:bool** - shows whether we got the Internet connectivity status when calling Nexus service (value true) or when calling generic web service API call (value false)</span></span>
